konse kapena kunyozedwa.

PAMENE Komalero anali mwana, anaona anthu alikugwira
nchito zosiyana-siyana, monga kulima, kumanga, kunya-
mula akatundu; kugulitsa zakudya, mphasa, mitanga
ndi nsengwa. Anaonanso ena alikugulitsa nyama, nkhuku,
mazira ndi nsomba. Anthu ena analikugulitsa nkhuni,
mitengo, nsungwi ndi mipini ya makasu. Ena anali
kupanga mipando, matebulo, makabati, mabedi ndi
zitseko. Komalero anaona anthu ena alikugwira nchito
m°maofesi a Azungu; anaonanso anthu ena alikulima
miseu, ena analikukonza nsapato za anthu. Anthu ena
analikusoka nsalu ndipo ena analikukonza njinga.
Koma mnyamatayu atayamba kukula, anapita ku sukulu
kukaphunzira pamodzi ndi anzace. Anamaliza kuphunzira,
ndipo sanalowe nchito msanga. Anayamba kuceza ndi
anthu onse amen analikugwira nchito zamitundu-
mitundu cifukwa anafuna kudziwa nzeru zosiyana-siyana.
Atayamba kuyendera anthu, anawafunsa kuti amuuze
ubwino wa nchito zao pamodzi ndi zobvuta zonse za
nchito. Komalero anafuna kudziwa nchito imene ipa-
mbana nchito zina zonse.
Anthu aja anamuuza kuti nchito iriyonse iri ndi
zobvuta zace pamodzi ndi zabwino zace; popanda
kupeza zobvuta pakugwira nchito, palibe zabwino. Ana-
muuza kuti zinthu zonse zabwino zicokera m'zobvuta ;
munthu aliyense amene agwira nchito ndi khama ndi
kusamala, adzalandira malipiro a nchito yace.

Mphunzitsi anauza Komalero kuti alowe m'nyumba
kuti akaceze bwino atakhala pa mipando. Pamene mnya-
matayo analowa m'nyumbamo mphunzitsi anamuuza kuti
akhale pa mpando waukulu. Komalero atakhala anapeza
kuti zokhalira za mpando zinali zofewa ndi zothandiza
thupi kupuma bwino. Maso ace sanathe kuyang'ana pa
malo amodzi, koma analikuyang'ana apa ndi apo mofu-
lumira. Anaona tebulo lalikulu labwino kwambiri ndipo
panali mipando isanu ndi umodzi kuzungulira tebulo ;

cipinda conse codyera ndipo mapazi a mnyamatayu

ndipo panalinso botolo
m'mene munali madzi ndi
maluwa abwino kwambiri. Khoma la cipindaco linali
loyeretsedwa ndi njereza, ndipo cithunzithunzi ca mphu-
nzitsi atakhala ndi mkazi wace ndi mwana wace cinali pa
khomapo cooneka mokoma ndithu. Panalinso kabati
lalikulu m'mene munali mbale, makapu ndi zinthu
zina zambiri. Tsopano Komalero anali ngati mlendo
amene anafika pa dziko lacilendo. Mkazi wa mphunzitsi
anali ndi nchito kupanga tii kuti amwe pamodzi ndi
mnyamata uja. Mkaziyo anabvala bwino ndi kugwira
nchito yace mofulumira. Anatsegula kabati ija ndi kutu-
lutsa mkaka, suga, keke, nthoci ndi malalanje ; zonse
anaziika pa tebulo, ndiponso anatulutsa makapu abwino
kwambiri ndi kuwaika pa tebulo pamodzi ndi tii. Onse atatu anayamba kumwa tii amene mkazi wa mphunzitsi
anamtsira m'makapu muja. Pakumwa til wabwino ndi
kudya keke amene anapanga mkazi wa mphunzitsi,
Komalero anayamba kukumbukira mau a kalaliki uja
amene ananena kuti iye apambana aphunzitsi ace onse
amene anamphunzitsa. Komalero anakumbukiranso kuti
kalaliki uja sanaceze naye m'nyumba mwace kuti aone

boma likondwera kwambiri pakuona anthu olima cifukwa

gwira nchito cifukwa liganiza kuti masiku onse tingo-
ganiza za kuba ndi kuononga zinthu zaeni. Monga

mpaka tsopano sindinayambe nchito; ndifuna kuyamba
nchito nditadziwa ubwino wa nchitoyo poyamba; ndiri
kuyenda-yenda kuceza ndi anthu ambiri kuti ndidziwe
wino cimene ndiyenera kucita. Lero ndifuna kudziwa
maganizo anu bambo.' Wolima uja anayankha, " Kooodi!
Lero ndikuuza kanthu; koma poyamba ndingofuna
kukudziwitsa kuti nthawi yonse imene unali pa sukulu,
unalikudya cakudya cimene Azungu a sukulu anagula
kwanga; aphunzitsi onse anadya cimanga canga, ndipo
m'mawa uliwonse Azungu ndi ena onse okhala pa sukulu anadya poliji wocokera m'cimanga canga. Palibe sukulu
limene lingatsegulidwe popanda cakudya cocokera kwa
mulimi monga ine. Popanda mulimi, nchito zonse rifa;
anthu afa ngati sadya cakudya, ndipo cakudya cicokera
m'kulima. Iwe Komalero wabwera kuno cifukwa wadya.
Ndalama zambiri za anthu a mitundu yonse zipita kwa
alimi masiku onse. Anthu onse, amuna ndi akazi ndi ana
adalira pa mulimi. Munthu sangathe kucenjera ndi
ndalama zace pa cakudya, koma azitulutsa ndithu ndi
kuzipereka kiwa mulimi. Ngati inu anyamata mufuna
kukhala anthu amphamvu ndi acuma, muyenera kukonda
nchito yakulima, ndipo khasu lidzakuphunzitsani zinthu
zambiri.
Komalero analibe mau ambiri, koma anangolankhula
mau otsika nati, ' Koma nchito yakulima ndiyo yadothi
ndithu, munthu wophunzira sangaoneke mokoma.' Mulimi
anayankha nati,
* Wophunzira aoneka bwino atadya
cakudya, ndiponso wophunzira ndiye munthu amene
angathe kuphunzitsa anthu ena malimidwe abwino
cifukwa anaphunzira njira zace pa sukulu.' (Tsopano
mulimi anauza Komalero kuti aone mbeu zonse zimene
zinalim'mundamo).
*Ona, uwu ndiwo munda waci-
manga, uwu wamapira, uwu wamawere ; ona mbatata

ukaone munda wanyemba zimene amagula Azungu a

Pamene Komalero anaona zinthu zonse, anakhutira

* Ndayendera anthu
ambiri ndi kuona nchito za0, koma nchito yanu yokha

Mulimi anadula nzimbe zitatu ndi kuzimanga mtolo

SAMWALI wa Komalero anaphunzira nchito yakupanga

siunaulekebeucitsiru??

anafika, ndipo aliyense analipira 5/-. Komalero anadabwa

zungu m'kabati pamodzi ndi makapu amagalasi awiri,

KOMALERO anafuna kuceza ndi munthu wosoka nsalu

nchito yotero. Makolo ace anali onyada kwambiri cifukwa
ca mwana wao wanzeru, ndipo onse anali olemera ku-
pambana mabanja a anthu ena.
Pakutha zaka zowerengeka, Komalero anayamba ku-
gulitsa mitengo, nkhuni ndi nsungwi. Cifukwa ca ici,

zimene anatha kuzipeza anazidzala ndi kuzioka. Tsopano
mnyamatayu analowa m'gulu la anthu odziwikä m'dziko
cifukwa ca nchito zace zazikulu zimene zinathandiza
anthu onse.

M°'KABUKHU aka muli nthano ya ufumu wa nyama.
Mfumu woyamba wa nyama anali mkango ; koma cifu-
kwa ca makhalidwe ace oipa, anabvuta nyama zonse
m'thengo pakuzipha ndi kuzidya. Nyama zinalibe mte-
ndere, ndipo masiku onse zinathawa ndi kuyesa kubisala,
komabe zambiri zinataya moyo wao cifukwa cakudya ca
mkango cinali nyama zokha masiku onse.
Mkango
unadwala, ndipo posacedwa unafa. Nyama zonse zinaika
maliro a mfumu m'manda ndi mitima yokondwa. Zina-
sankha mfumu watsopano amene zinaganiza kuti adzazi-
sunga bwino. Mfumu watsopanoyu anali njobvu.
Pakuwerenga nthanoyi, mudzaona kuti maina onse
a nyama alembedwa ndi zilembo zazikulu poyamba cifu-
kwa nthano yao ndinaisandutsa ngati ya anthu, ndipo
maina ao akhalanso ngati a anthu.
Nthanoyi ndailembera ana kuti akondwe pakumva
zimene zinacitika ndi ufumu wa nyama, komanso akulu
angathe kuwerenga ndi kumva za ufumu umenewu.

NYAMA zonse zitalengedwa zinalibe mfumu. Tsiku lina,
zone zinasonkhana pamodzi kuti zipangane ndi kusankha
mfumu wao wamkulu. Nyama zazikulu zinafunsa kuti,
" Ndani adzakhala mfumu wa ife tonse kuti atisunge ndi
kutiweruza? Koma nyama zonse zinali kuopa mkango
cifukwa ca ukali wace ndi mphamu zace, ndipo zina-
funa kuti mkango ukhale mfumu wao.
Nyama zina
sizinafune kuti mkango ukhale mfumu, cifukwa unapha
nyama ndi kuzidya masiku onse. Nyama izi zinasankha
Njobvu; zina zinakana cifukwa Njobvu inali yaikulu ndi
yonenepa kwambiri kotero kuti siingathe kuthamanga ndi
kumenya nkhondo ngati amaliwongo abwera m'dziko
la nyama. Nyama zina zinanena kuti Njobvu iri yofatsa
kwambiri ndipo siingathe kulamula ndi mphamvu, ndipo
ufumu wace udzakhala wopanda mphamvu, nyama
sizidzaiopa ndi kuimvera.
Nkhani yakusankha mfumu inali yaikulu ndi yobvuta,
ndipo inatenga masiku ambiri kuikamba, cifukwa nyama
zinafuna kupeza mfumu wabwino.
'Tsopano nyama
zonse zinabvomera kuti Mango ukhale mfumu. Mkango
unakondwera kwambiri cifukwa unadziwa kuti udzapha
ndi kudya nyama popanda cobvuta. Koma nyama zonse
zinakhulupira kuti Mango udzaleka kupha nyama ndi
kuzidya cifukwa palibe mfumu amene apha ndi kudya
anthu ace.

PAMENE Mkango unasankhidwa kukhala mfumu, nyama
zonse zinakonza caka cacikulu. Zinaphika zakudya zami-
tundu-mitundu ndi kukonza zakumwa zambiri zokoma ;
nyama zina zinakonza nyimbo ndi masewera osiyana-
siyana ambiri.
Tsiku la caka litafika, nyama zonse
zocokera uku ndi uko zinasonkhana pa bwalo labwino
ndi lalikulu,
Zinaitana Mango pamodzi ndi abale ace
onse kuti aone kubveka ufumu.
Pamene Mkango
unafika pa bwalo ndi abale ace, Njobvu inatenga cipewa
ca ufumu ndi kupfuula kuuza nyama zone, kuti,
"Onani
nonse, Mango ndiye mfumu wathu wamkulu amene
adzatiyang'anirandikutiweruza;
if tonse tiyenera
kumvera ndi kumulemekeza kwambiri! '
Ndipo nyama
zamphongo, zazikazi pamodzi ndi ana, zinaomba m'manja
ndi kupfuula,
"Zikomo kwambiri, tiri okondwa paku-
khala ndi mfumu tsopano!
Nyama zazikazi zinayamba kuimba nyimbo zokoma
ndi kubvina. Mau a nyimbo anali mwambo kuphunzitsa
mfumu wao kuti akhale ndi makhalidwe abwino ndi
nzeru. Mau a nyimbo anali otere :
" Tifuna mfumu wopanda tsankho,
Tsankho lipasula dziko,
Mfumu wanzeru akweza anthu ace popanda nsanje,
Ukapha anthu ako umwaza dziko.'
Mfumu Mkango anamva mwambo wonse umene nyama zinalalika pa bwalo.
Mwambo utatha, mfumu analowa
m'nkhalango ndi kubangula kuti,
* Dzikoli ndi langa, ndi
langa, ndi langa! '
Amaliwongo atamva mau oopsawo,
anaopa kulowa m'dziko la nyama, cifukwa anali mau
ocititsa mantha ndithu. Mauwo anagwedeza dziko lonse
lapansi.

KoMA mfumu MIkango anacita cinthu coipa cacikulu pa
nthawi ya ufumu wace.
Anapha nyama zambiri ndi
kuzidya.
Cakudya cace cinali nyama zokha.
Nyama
zinaopa mfumu wao ndi kukwiya kwambiri.
Pamene
zinamva mfumu Mkango ali kubangula, zonse zinathawa
ndi kubisala m'thengo m'nkhalango zazikulu.
Nyama
zinalibe mtendere, ndipo sizinakhale pafupi ndi mfumu wao. Mfumu woopsayo anayenda ndi mkazi wace ndi
ana ace ndi abale ace, osati ndi nyama zina.
'Tsiku lina mfumu Mkango anafuna kugwira ndi kupha
Mmbulu.
Koma Mmbulu uli ndi maonekedwe ngati
galu, ndipo uli ndi mphamvu kuposa Mango. Nkhondo
yoopsa inayamba, ndipo Mmbulu unaluma mfumu
Mkango ndi kumpweteka. Mkango unapita ku phanga
lace ndi kudwala, ndipo posacedwa unafa.
Nyama
zinasonkhana pa maliro a mfumu, koma zinalibe cisoni
m'mitima; zinakondwa cifukwa mfumu woipayo anafa.
Zitatha kuika maliro, nyama zazikulu zinakambirana,
ndipo zinapeza kuti zidzasankha mfumu wa mtundu
wina osati Mkango wina; zinanena kuti Mikango yonse
inali yoipa cifukwa siikonda cakudya ca mtundu wina,
koma nyama yokha. Koma Mikango inakhulupira kuti
ufumu wa mbale wao udzalowanso m'manja mwao,
siinadziwe zimene nyama zone zinapangana.
Inadzi-
tama ponse-ponse kuti ufumu udzakhala wa Mikango
nthawi zonse cifukwa panalibe nyama ina yocenjera ndi
yaukali monga Mikango.

PAMENE nyama zinatha kulira maliro a mfumu Mkango,
zinayamba kukamba nkhani ya kusankha mfumu watso-
pano. Zinasonkhana pa bwalo; nyama zoyenera kusa-nkhidwa kukhala mfumu zinachulidwa kuti imodzi mwa
izo isankhidwe kukhala mfumu,
Nyama zimene zina-
chulidwa zinali, Njobvu, Njati, Pembere, Fisi ndi Nchefu.
Koma Mvuu anagwira nchito yakusankha mfumu mwa
nyama zisanuzo.
Mvuu analamula kuti nyama zosa-
nkhidwazo zikhale iriyonse payokha, ndipo kuti nyama
iriyonse imene ikonda imodzi mwa zisanuzo kukhala
mfumu, ¡pite kukakhala pa malo pamene nyamayo
yakhala. Nyama zonse zinathamanga, ndipo iriyonse
inakhala pa malo pamene inakhala nyama imene anai-
konda kukhala mfumu. Cinthu cokondweretsa cinaoneka
kwa Njobvu, cifukwa nyama zambiri zinapita kwa iye.
Nyama zina zinapita kwa Nchefu.
Ng'ombe inapita
kwa Njati cifukwa anadziwana kwambiri.
Nyani,
Mphaka, khandwe ndi Nyalugwe anakwiya cifukwa
panalibe mmodzi mwa iwo anachulidwa pa ufumu.
Pembere analibe bwenzi m'dziko la nyama cifukwa masiku
onse anali ndi makhalidwe oipa.
Ciwerengero ca nyama zofuna Njobvu cinafanafana ndi
ca Nchefu.
Mvuu anapfuula kuuza nyama zonse,
" Ciwerengero ca anthu awiri ciri colingana ; koma
sitingathe kukhala ndi mafumu awiri pa dziko limodzi !
Nyama zimene zinafuna Nchefu zinayankha,
Tifuna
Nchefu cifukwa ali wofatsa, ndipo siaba cimanga
ca
anthu m'minda yao!'
Myuu anafunsa nyama zija
zimene zinasankha Njobvu, anati
" Cifukwa ciani inu
mufuna Njobvu kuti akhale mfumu ?
Nyama zija
zinayankha,
' Tifuna Njobvu cifukwa ali wofatsa ndi
wamkulu, ndipo nyama zonse zidzamuopa ndi kumu-lemekeza!
Nyama zimene zinafuna Nchefu zinati,
'Njobvu imadya zone zimene izipeza m'minda ya anthu
popanda kupempha, conco sitifuna mfumu wotero.'
Nthawi yomweyo nyama zimene zinali pa mbali ya
Njobvu, zinapfuulanso kuti,
* Nchefu anadya thonje
m'minda ya anthu ; anthu anadzala thonje kuti adzaombe
nsalu ndi kupanga zobvala zamitundu-mitundu, ndipo
Nchefu ndi banja lace lonse anadya thonje lone ; masiku
one Nchefu ayenda-yenda kufunafuna thonje m'minda.'
Nyama zija
zinapitirira
kulankhula, zinati,
Tifuna
Njobvu cifukwa adzatha kuyang'anira nyama zonse
m'nkhalango osazibvuta monga anali kucita mfumu
woipa uja Mango ;
,ngati mfumu Njobvu adzadya
cimanga ca anthu m'minda, adzamulasa ndi uta ndi
mibvi cifukwa ca kupusa kwace.
Njobvu anasanduka mfumu wa nyama zone, ndipo
Nchefu anasankhidwa kukhala nduna ya mfumu. Nyama
zazikulu ndi zanzeru zinalangiza akulu awiri awa kuti
agwire bwino nchito ya ufumu. Mikango yonse inakwiya
cifukwa ufumu unacoka m'manja mwao ndi kulowa
m°manja mwa Njobvu.

NjoBvU atalandira ufumu, anaitana nyama zazikulu kuti
zimthandize kusankha athandizi ena. Pa msonkhano wao
anasankha Pembere kuti akhale mkulu woyang'anira asikali ankhondo amene adzamenyana ndi adani ofuna
kulowa m'dziko la nyama.

Nchito ya Mvuu idzakhala yakulonda madoko
onse a nyanja kuti amaliwongo asaoloke ndi kulowa
m'dziko. Nyalugwe anakhala msikali womenya nkhondo
ndi manja cifukwa ali ndi zala zakuthwa. Koma Njati
cifukwa ca mutu wace waukulu ndi wolimba, adzamenya
nkhondo pakugundana ndi adani.
Njiri analandira
nchito yophunzitsa kulima cifukwa adziwa kukumba
pansi kufunafuna cakudya. Ngoma anasankhidwa kuti
akhale wotumikira mfumu pakuthamanga ndi mithenga
ndi makalata cifukwa ali ndi myendo yaitali.
Mfumu Njobvu analamula Ng'ombe, Nkhumba ndi
Mbuzi kuti zipite kukhala ndi anthu m'midzi cifukwa
ngati zikhala m'thengo, Mikango ija imene iri yokwiya,
idzazipha ndi kuzidya cifukwa ziribe mphamvu kume-
nyana nayo.
Galu anapitanso kukakhala ndi anthu
m'midzi, cifukwa ngati akhala m'thengo adzayamba
kuuwa pamene adzaona mfumu Njobvu alikupita kuona
dziko lace, ndipo ngati nyama zidzamva kuuwa, kwa
galu, zidzaganiza kuti galuyo ali kuuwa cifukwa waona
nkhondo ya adani athu; pakutero, nyama zonse zidza-
yamba kuthawa ndi kukonzekera nkhondo. Galu ayenera
kuthandiza anthu ndi kuwacenjeza ngati Afisi ndi
Mikango zibwera m'midzi kudzabvuta anthu.

MPUMU Njobvu atalandira ufumu ndi kusankha athandizi
ace ndi kuwapatsa nchito zao, anaika malamulo oyenera
kuwasunga nyama iriyonse m'dziko.
Mfumu anati,
* Ndirikuthokoza
inu nonse cifukwa mwandisankha
kukhala mfumu wanu wamkulu. Ine sindinaganize konse
kuti ndidzakhala mfumu, koma cifukwa inu mwandi-
khulupirira kuti ndidzagwira bwino nchito yanga ya
ufumu, tsopano ndiri mfumu.
Koma tonse tiyenera
kukondana ndi kuthandizana nthawi zone; tinalandira
udzu ndi masamba m'thengo lathu, ndipo aliyense
ayenera kudya zimenezo, osapha ndi kudya nyama
zinzathu.
Tiri ndi zipatso zambiri m'dziko lathu, ndipo
amene akonda zipatsozo, angathe kuzidya cifukwa ziri
m'dziko lathu ndipo ziri zathu. Ambuye amene anatilenga
anatikonda pakutipatsa zipatso ndi zakudya zina zosabvu-
ta kuzipeza. Koma amene afuna zipatso ayenera kupe-
mpha Nyani cifukwa ndiye adziwa kukwera mitengo,
koma amene afuna zakudya zokhala pansi m'nthaka,
afunse Njiri, ndipo adzamthandiza kukumba ndi kuzi-
peza.
Mfumu
anapitirirabekulankhula,
" Ngati nkhondo
ilowa m'dziko lathu, nyama iriyonse iyenera kugwira
nchito molimba mtima ndi kukhonjetsa mdani ; koma
nyama
imene idzakhala yofooka,
idzaphedwa
ndi
amaliwongo.'
Mfumu anacenjeza nyama zone kuti, 'Popeza kuti ufumu wacotsedwa m'banja la Mikango,
cenjerani ; sungani ana anu bwino kuti asaphedwe ndi
Mikangoyo. Koma dziwani bwino kuti Mikango siingathe
kugwira ndi kupha ana anga, cifukwa itayesa kutero,
ndidzaigwira ndi citamba canga ndi kuimenyetsa ku
mitengo.'
Mfumu ananena za mitengo nati,
" Samalani bwino
mitengo cifukwa
imatithandizakupangankhalango
m'mene tikhala ndi kubisala. . Adani athu ena aopa
kulowa m'nkhalango cifukwa siatha kuona kutali, ndipo-
no siangathe kuthawa pamene ife tikalipa kwambiri ndi
kuwathamangitsa.'

MFUMU anakonza banja lace kuti likhale ndi makhalidwe
amodzimodzi ndi kukhala pamodzi nthawi zone. Anala-
mula mkazi wace kuti asamale ana ace osawalola kupita
kutali. Anamuuza kuti ana ace asalongolole ndi ana a
nyama zina, koma ayanjane ndi ana a nyama zonse
•cifukwa ive analowa ufumu kuti asamale nyama zonse.
Ananena kuti mkazi wace pamodzi ndi ana ace, asame-
nyane ndi Mango uliwonse, cifukwa ngati acita conco,
adzawawitsa mitima ya Mikango yonse cifukwa Mikango
irikulira ufumu wao. Mfumu analankhula mopfuula kwa
mkazi wace,
* Sindifuna zobvuta pakati pa ine ndi
Mikango! Koma ngati Mikango idzalakalaka kume-nyana ndi ana anga, sindidzaleka kuibwezera cipongwe
cao.
Kuyambira nthawi imeneyi Njobvu zonse zinakhala pa
gulu limodzi pa banja lao m'nkhalango. M'gulu lao,
mfumu anasankha Njobvu yaukali imene anaichula dzina
lace Nyungwa.
Nyungwa ndiyo Njobvu yaukali ndi
yamphamvu, ndiponso yopanda minyanga,
Mikango
inaopa ndithu osayesa kusewera ndi ana a mfumu
jobvu, cifukwa Nyungwa inateteza gulu lonse. Ndipo
mpaka lero, pa gulu lirilonse la Njobvu pali Nyungwa
amene asunga ndi kuteteza gulu lonse kwa amaliwongo.
Ngati munthu afuna kupha Njobvu ndi mfuti ayenera
kusamala, cifukwa Njobvu iyi ingathe kumgwira ndi
kummenyetsa kumtengo.

MIKANGO inakwiya ndi kudana ndi nyama zonse cifukwa
zinasankha Njobvu kukhala mfumu.
Komabe Mikango
siinadane ndi mfumu Njobvu cifukwa inaopa. Mikango
yonse inaganiza kuti idzapita m'thengo lone ndi kuba-
ngula ndi mau amphamvu kudziwitsa nyama ndi zole-
ngedwa zirizonse kuti ufumu siunacoke m'manja mwa
Mikango.
Mkango uliwonse unabangula kwambir
masiku onse kuti, * Dzikoli ndanga ! Ndanga ! Ndanga !
Pakumva nyama zone, zinaganiza kuti ufumu uj unabwezedwa kwa Mikango;
koma Mvuu amene
anagwira nchito yakusankha mfumu tsiku lija, anaziuza
kuti ufumu siunacoke ndi kubwezedwa kwa Mikango,
koma uli m'manja mwa Njobvu. Mikango inangopfuula
cifukwa ca manyazi. Anthu anadziwanso kuti Mikango
sindiyo mafumu anyama; koma cifukwa ca ukali wa
Mikango ndi kuopsa kwao, anthu anaopa Mikango
kupambana Njobyu mfumu wa nyama zonse.
Lero Mikango imayenda uku ndi uko kukalalika za
ufumu wao, ndipo nyama zikamva kupfuula koopsako,
zimathawa ndi kukabisala m°'nkhalango zazikulu. Kumene
kuli Njobvu, Mikango sikhalako cifukwa ca cidani ca
ufumu. Nyama zikamva fungo la Mikango, zithawa;
koma Njobvu ikaona Mkango, ingoganiza kuti ndi
kanthu kakang'ono.

MPUMU analamula kuti Mimbulu ikakhale ndi anthu
m'midzi ndi kuwathandiza monga acita galu.
Koma
Mimbulu itakhala nthawi pang'ono ndi anthu, inaganiza
kuti kutero sikunali kwabwino.
Mimbulu inanena kuti
Mbuzi ziri zopusa kwambiri, ndiponso galu ali wacipo-
ngwe cifukwa ca kuuwa kwace.
Mimbulu inayamba
kumenyana ndi Mbuzi, ndipo Mbuzi zambiri zinaphedwa.
Anthu anapsa mtima ndi kuithamangitsa kuti ibwerere ku
thengo kwao.

Pamene Mimbulu inabwerera kwao ku thengo, sinaya-
njanenso ndi nyama zonse. Mimbulu inakhala pa banja
lao ndipo inapha nyama ndi kuzidya masiku onse.
Maliro anamveka ponse-ponse m'dziko la nyama, ndipo
mabanja onse a nyama anamwazikana kuthawa Mimbulu
yobvutayo. Mfumu Njobvu anamva za zobvuta izi,
ndipo anaitana Mimbulu yonse kuti adzaifunse cifukwa
cimene inacokera ku midzi. Mimbulu inakana kukamva
mau a mfumu.
Masiku onse inabisala m'maudzu ndi
kupha nyama zambiri.
Tsiku lina Mimbuluyo inamva Mkango ulikubangula
kuti,
" Ndanga!
Ndanga!
Ndanga!'
Pamenepo
zobvuta zinaoneka.
Mango ndi Mimbulu zinathama-
ngitsana kopambana, ndipo Mango unathamanga liwiro
lodabwitsa ndi loseketsa. Mango umene unapfuula kuti
dzikoli ndi lace, unathawa liwiro lapfumbi.
Ndipo
kufikira lero, Mikango silyanjana ndi Mimbulu ; Mikango
ikadziwa kuti Mimbulu iri pafupi, ingothawiratu zisa-
naonane ndi kukabisala kutali.

NYALUGWE anamva kuti msuwani wace Mango anapeza
zobvuta tsiku lina pamene Mimbulu inamthamangitsa.
lye
anafuna kuonana ndi Mimbulu
ndi kumva
cifukwa ciani inafuna kumwetula msuwani wace.
Tsiku lina anakomana ndi Mmbulu
umodzi wamphongo.
Nyalugwe anafunsa mwaukali,
" Cifukwa ciani iwe una-
funa kumwetula msuwani wanga? Lero uona kanthu ;
ndikukanda ndi nchala zanga zakuthwa, ndipo ubvutika
ndi mabala oopsa.

Mmbulu unayankha,
" Iwe Nyalugwe, ngati siunako-
mane ndi zobvuta cikhalire, lero uona kanthu; matumbo
ako aoneka panja, ndipo nchenche zidzakhala ndi
phwando lalikulu kudya matumbowo.' Pompo nkhondo
inayamba, nkhondo imene siinaonekenso kale. Nyalugwe
anathamanga kuti abisale
m'maudzu aatali, koma
Mmbulu unamtsata manga ulikuuwa, Nyalugwe sianathe ngakhale kupuma pakudziwa kuti cirombo camphamvu
cinali pambuyo pace.
'Tsopano Mmbulu unayandikira
pafupi ndi Nyalugwe ndi kummwetula pamsana. Pame-
nepo Nyalugwe anaonjeza liwiro lenileni kuthyola udzu
ndi zitsamba, ndipo anapeza mtengo ndi kulumpha
kukwera.
Mmbulu unalephera kukwera mtengowo.
Unayang'ana Nyalugwe uja, unati,
"Iwe Nyalugwe,
ucenjere; ngati siusamala udzafa posacedwa; ndidza-
kudya wosaphika ndi kumwa magazi ako onse.
Pamene Mmbulu unacoka, Nyalugwe anathokoza
Mulungu amene anampulumutsa. Anaganiza kuti aye-
nera kuphunzitsa abale ace onse kuti asamasewera ndi
Mimbulu,
Tsopano abale ace a
Nyalugwe anaphunzira
za
Mimbulu, ndipo sangasewere nayo.

ZOBVUTA zonse
zimene zinaoneka pamene Mkango,
Nyalugwe ndi Mmbulu anathamangitsana, Fisi sianazi-
dziwe.
Monga tidziwa kuti Fisi amalephera kawiri-
kawiri kugwira nyama, iye amangotola nyama zobvunda
zimene Mimbulu, Mikango ndi Anyalugwe anazisiya
atakhuta.
Tsiku lina Fisi anadzuka m'mawa;
anapita kufupi
ndi mudzi kukatola mafupa amene anataya. Koma tsiku limeneli sianapeze matupa.
Dzuwa linayamba kutuluka
ndipo Fisi anaopa kuti kapena anthu adzamuona. Ana-
bwerera manga kupita kuthengo alikuthamanga.
Ata-
lowa m'thengo, anamva pfungo la magazi a nyama, ndipo
anima kuti atsate bwino kumene kunacokera kapfungo
kaja.
Anayenda, ndipo posacedwa anafika pa malo
pamene Mimbulu inapha Mbawala.
Mimbuluyo ina-
gona pansi kupuma pa mbali ina.
Fisi uja sianayambe
kuona kuti adziwe cimene cinapha Mbawala, koma ana-
ngoyamba kumwa magazi ndi kutola mafupa ndi zina
zotsala,
Mimbulu inakalipa ndi kuyamba kumthama-ngitsa. Inu mukanakhala pafupi nthawi imeneyo, muka-
naonadi kuti kunali kuthamanga kwamphamvu m'mau-
dzumo.
Udzu ndi zitsamba zimene zinali pa njira,
zinazulidwa.
Kunali kuthamanga kwa imfa.
Fisi atayamba kutopa anaganiza kuti njira yabwino
inali yothawira ku phanga lalikulu kumene anali kugona.
Koma atafika pafupi ndi phanga lace, Mmbulu wina
wocenjera unadutsa kutsogolo, ndipo Fisi analephera
kulowa ku phanga lace.
Pamene anafuna kuthawira
kwina, Mmbulu wina unazula mcira wa Fisi ndi kuudya
nthawi yomweyo.
Pamenepo panali mabvuto aakulu
kwa Fisi. Mumtima mwace anaganiza kuti akanapanda
kutsata fungo lija la magazi, zonsezo sizikanaoneka,
Nthawi imeneyi Fisi sianali kuna kumene anayenera
kuthawira, popeza kuti Mimbulu inamuyandikira pafupi.
Mmbulu umene unalawa mcira uja siunafune kumsiya
Fisi wosusukayo.
Fisi anatopa ndipo anamgwira ndi
kumpha.
Mimbulu inamdya Fisi osatsala ngakhale
mafupa ace. Uku ndiko kutha kwa moyo wa Fisi amene
anafera fungo la magazi a Mbawala.

NCHITO ya Mbidzi inali yophunzitsa nyama zonse
nkhondo yomenya ndi myendo cifukwa iye anadziwa
nchito imeneyi kwambiri. Ngati Mbidzi akwiya, palibe nyama iriyonse ingathe kumuyandikira.
Tsiku lina
Mango unakomana ndi gulu lalikulu la Ambidzi, ndipo
iwo unaganiza kuti udzadya nyama yofewa ndi yonu-
nkhira. Unathamangitsa gulu lonselo. Ambidzi anatha-
manga pamodzi mokometsera ngati akavalo.
Anafika
pa phiri pamene panali myala yambiri ndipo anaponya
myala ija ndi myendo yao mwamphamvu.
Myala ya-
mbiri inamenya Mango, koma iwo siunasamale. Unafika
pafupi ndi Mbidzi wamkulu, koma Mbidzi anaukankha
ndi mwendo kwambiri.
Mkango siunafunenso kume-
nyana ndi Mbidzi; unathawa cifukwa manu ace anali
kupweteka. Pamene Mbidzi anaona Mkango uli kuthawa,
anapfuula,
" Iwe, pita ukauze abale ako onse kuti asayese
konse kusewera ndi ife cifukwa sitifuna cibwana.' Pamene unafika kwa abale, unawauza kuti kusewera ndi Mbidzi
ndiko kulakwa kwambiri; tingathe kupha Mbidzi ngati
timpeza atagona. Nyama ya Mbidzi iri yonunkhira ndi
yofewa, koma kuli kobvuta kupha Mbidzi ngati iye ali
wokonzeka.

PEMBERE anakhala mkulu wotsogolera ndi kulamulira
nkhondo.
Iye akonda kumenyana cifukwa ali waukali
ndi wamphamvu. Pembere atakalipa, m'mphuno mwace
mutuluka mamina. Ngati apeza kuti anthu akoleza moto
pa thengo, iye amwaza motowo ndi ukali ndi kuononga
akatundu a anthuwo. Atamva mfuti kulira, iye athama-
ngira kumeneko kukathyola mfutiyo, ndipo anthu osaka
nyama athawa.
Pamene mfumu Njobvu anasankha Pembere kukhala
mkulu wa askali, mfumu anasankha bwino ndithu cifukwa
Pembere ali woyeneradi pa nchito ya nkhondo. Pembere
anagawa askali ace m'magulu osiyana ndipo pa gulu
lirilonse panali mtsogoleri wace. Nyalugwe anali mkulu
wa askali oyenda pansi cifukwa iye adziwa kubisala
m'thengo. Nyani anal mtsogoleri wa azondi oyang'ana
ngati adani alikubwera cifukwa adziwa kukwera mitengo
yaitali ndi kuona kutali. Njati anakhala mkulu wa askali
omenya nkhondo pakugundana ndi mitu popeza kuti mutu wace uli waukulu ndi wolimba. Mvuu anakhala
mlonda wa pa nyanja kuona kuti amaliwongo asaoloke
ndi kulowa m'dziko la nyama.
Pembere analamulira bwino askali ace.
Iye mwini
anayenda m'nkhalango kuona ngati nchito zone zinali
kuyenda bwino.
Atayenda ulendo wautali, Pembere
anali kubwerera pa njira yomweyo ali kuthamanga
kwambiri kuti ngati adani anali kumtsata, awamwaze
ndi mphamvu.

MFUNU Njobvu anati,
' Iwe Mvuu, udzasunga gulu la
askali olonda pa nyanja ndi pa mitsinje yonse ndi kuona
kuti amaliwongo asaoloke.
Ngati iwe ndi askali ako
muona kuti adani alikufuna kuoloka, muyenera kuuza
Pembere manga kuti iye atumize magulu a nkhondo
kukabweza adaniwo.
Pita ukasonkhanitse Mvuu zonse
ndi kuziuza ndi kuzipatsa malo kulonda. Mwezi uliwo-
nse uyenera kudziwitsa Pembere zone zimene zaoneka
pa mweziwo. Koma popeza kuti anthu a dziko lino ali
ndi minda yao m'mene amalima ndi kudzala mbeu za0,
sindifuna kudzamva kuti wina wa inu anaba ndi kudya
cimanga ca anthu. Mukacita conco, ife tonse tidzakhala
ndi nkhondo ndi anthu ndipo adzatiombera mfuti. Amene
adzaba cimanga ca anthu, ndidzamulanga koopsa ndithu.

Mvuu inabvomera,
" Inde mfumu ndamva, ndipo
ndikasonkhanitsa askali anga onse ndi kuwauza mala-
mulo anu.'- Myuu itapita, inasonkhanitsa askali ace onse
ndi mabanja ao ndi kuwauza malamulo a mfumu, Mvuu
zonse zinadandaula kuti,
* Cifukwa ciani inu mtsogoleri
wathu mwabvomera malamulo onse a mfumu, maka-
maka lamulo loletsa kudya cimanga m'minda ? Kodi
mfumu adzatipatsa phoso lotani?
Ife tikonda kudya
zambiri, kodi" mfumul
cimanga caciwisi, nzimbe, nthoci ndi zina
adzatipatsa zonsezi?
Ngati
sitidzalandira zakudya zotere, tidzadya mbeu zirizonse
zimene tidzazipeza pafupi ndi nyanja kapena mitsinje,
ndipo sitidzaonekera pa maso pa mfumu.'
Mvuu mtsogoleri wao anabvomerezana nao, ndipo
anawauza kuti acite monga afuna; anawauzanso kuti
ngati mfumu adzatuma askali ace kudzatigwira, ife tonse tidzamira m'madzi kubisala,
Conco nchito ya Mvuu
inatha, panalibe askali olonda pa nyanja.
Kuyambira thawi imeneyo, Mvuu zonse zikhala
m'madzi; usiku zituluka ndi kukadya mbeu za anthu
m'minda imene iri pafupi. Sizifuna kuonana ndi Njobru
cifukwa ziopa mlandu uja wokana lamulo la mfumu.
Komanso ngakhale Njobvu inalamula nyama zone kuti
risaononge mbeu za anthu, Njobvu imalawira m'mawa
kukadya cimanga ndi mbeu zina za anthu m'minda yao
ndi kubwereranso ku nkhalango.
Anthu ataona kuti
Njobvu pamodzi ndi abale ace anadya mbeu zao, azitsata.
M°'njira apeza ndowe zambiri pamodzi ndi cimanga,
maungu ndi mbeu zina zimene Njobvu zinadya. Njobvu
sizitafuna cakudya cao, koma zingomeza zathunthu, ndipo
zonsezo zipezeka m'ndowe zao, makamaka zakudya
zolimba zimene sizingathe kupukusika m'mimba.

PEMBERE mkulu wa askali anauza Nyani kuti adzilonda
nkhalango zonse pamodzi ndi askali ace ndi kuna kuti
adani asalowe. Anamuuza kuti ngati aona adani aliku-
bwera, apfuule manga ndipo Pembere adzatumiza askali
kukakomana ndi amaliwongowo.
Nyani analemba askali ambiri a mtundu wace ndi
kuwapatsa nkhalango ndi mapiri kuti akhalemo ndi kulonda,
Iwo anakwera m'mitengo ndi kuyang'ana
kutali usiku ndi usana. Maso ao anayamba kuya cifukwa
ca kuyang'ana kwambiri, ndiponso cifukwa ca njala;
ananda kwambiri kufikira nkhope zao ndi milomo yao
zinaoneka ngati anadwala caka cathunthu.
Nthawi
yacirimwe, udzu wonse unapsa, ndipo panalibe cakudya.
Atayang'ana kutali anaona masamba obiriwira, bango ndi
zina, ndipo anaganiza za kupitako. Anatsika pansi, koma
pansi panali phulusa lokha la udzu (lupsa). Anayenda
pa lupsa. Manja ao anada kwambiri. Pamene anafika
pa mtsinje, anapeza madzi, ndipo anasamba m'manja, koma m'manja
mwao simunayere cifukwa anayenda
ulendo wautali alikuponda phulusa.
Anaona minda ya cimanga caciwisi; anayamba kuba
cimanga, ndipo sanabwererenso ku nchito yao. Masiku
one anayenda ulendo wautali kufunafuna cimanga ndi
mbeu zina m'minda ya anthu. Lero anthu alikubvutika
ndi Anyani m'minda, nyama zobvuta kopambana. Tsiku
lina anthu anathamangitsa Anyani ndi agalu ao, koma
Nyani wina wamkulu anagwira galu ndi kumuluma
kwambiri pa mana. Galu anathawa ali ndi bala lalikulu
tsopano agalu sasewera ndi Nyani cifukwa ali kuopa.

NCHITO ya Nyalugwe inali yomenyana ndi adani pakuwa-
tsatira m'thengo. Anaphunzitsa anzace onse njira yaku-
menya nkhondo m'nkhalango kuti pamene ali kuyenda,
asaonetse bande kapena khwalala kudziwitsa kuti iwo
apita, koma kuyenda osathyola udzu.
Anawaphunzitsa-
no kuti ngati agwira mdani, nthawi zonse adzimgwira
pa khosi ndi kumdula manga ndi zala zao zakuthwa.
Anyalugwe onse anaphunzira kugwira pa khosi nthawi
ya nkhondo.
Koma anaopa Mmbulu masiku onse
cifukwa tsiku lija anammwetula pa msana, ndipo
sianaiwale zija zinaoneka tsiku limenelo.
" Kodi
mwamva
ambuye?
Nyalugwe
wagwira mbuzi ya mfumu, ndipo wangoidula pa khosi.'
Anthu
anathamanga ndi nthungo,
mauta ndi nkhwangwa.
Anampeza alikudya mbuzi ija, ndipo pamene anaona
anthu aja, anathawa ndi kulowa pa thengo. Anthu ana-
mtsatabe, ndipo atampeza anamulasa ndi nthungo.
Nyalugwe anakalipa kwambiri nalumpha ndi kukanda
munthu amene anamulasa uja.
Tsopano Nyalugwe
anayamba kukanda munthu aliyense amene anamuona,
ndipo anthu onse anathawa kupita ku mudzi ali ndi
mabala pa khosi, pa mana, pa mimba ndi pa mutu.
Usiku, Nyalugwe wina anapita ku mudzi kwa anthu
aja amene analasa mbale wace.
Galu anamva msanga
pfungo la Nyalugwe uja, ndipo anayamba kuuwa. Nya-
lugwe anapsa mtima.
Anathamanga ndi kugwira galu
wacipongweyo.
Anampha ndi kupita naye ku thengo
kukamdya.
Kumeneko anakomana ndi Nyalugwe uja
amene anthu anamulasa ndi nthungo, ndipo onse awiri
anadya nyama yonona.
Kuyambira tsiku limeneli,
Nyalugwe atabwera m'mudzi ayamba kufunafuna galu.
Anyalugwe onse analeka nchito ija yausikali, koma ango-
gwira mbuzi, nkhumba, agalu ndi nkhuku m'midzi.
Nyalugwe atagwira mbuzi, anthu aopa kumtsata cifukwa
ali kukumbukirabe mabala aja.

New book

Malingaliro omwe ndagwiritsira ntchito m’nkhaniyi ndidawapeza kuchokera m’kuchere kwanga ndi mnzanga Wapamtima.
Benedicto Wokomaatani Malunga yemwe ndi munthu wotchuka kwambiri pa luntha lolemba ndakatulo, “
Nthawi zina n’kwapafupi kuwerenga nthano ndi kuitenga ngati nkhani yopeka chabe.
Ndifuna Kulupemphani awerengi keuti ngakhale zomwe ndalemba m’bukhu la ‘Idzani Muone’ ndi zochokera m'mutu.
chingakhale chinthu chothandise mutaitenga nkhaniyi mozama ndi kugwirizana nane kuti zoterezi zikhozadi kuchitika kwa munthe yemwe moyo wake ngothamangathamanga.
Mkazi wanga Annie nat anzanga awa:- Andrea Donner (wa ku Holland, koma adagwirapo ntchito kuno ku Malawi) ndi Eric Mabedi
mnyamata wotchuka Pamasewera azisudzo, adandithandiza kwambiri Patsutsana mane mu zina ndi zina.
Kuchokera m’kutsutsana kumeneku ndidakonza mwina momwe Poyamba simudali kumveka bwino.
Sinditha kutchula maina 2 awerengi a mabuku anga omwe kawirikawiri amandiyimitsa pamsewu.
kapena kubwera kunyumba kwange ndi malangizo a momwe ndingapitirizire patsogolo nichito yolembayi.
Abale ndi alongo dziwani kuti ndinu a mtengo wapatali.
Popanda inu ndiye kuti kulemba kwanga kulibe phindu.
Zikomo kwambiri.
Kudera Ja nyanja yaikulu dzina lake Maji ndi malo otentha kwambiri.

Akutitu kalelo ku Mondwe munthu wina atafa adadzauka mkango.

Ana akhanda inu nkuyamwa komwe simudasiye.

Kodi ina mukuyean kuti poynmiba deine ais ‘dali Chipolopolo?
Daina lake lenilent lidaalt Bene ‘Wadi Macheso, Ii la Chipolopolo lidayamba nthawi ya tkhondo ya Ajeremani.
Achimwene, akuti nkhondo itavutamunthu wine adawauza Ajeremani kuti apite Kwa‘g'anga yachikuda yomwe idali ndi mankhwala oti chipolopolo kulasa osalowa pathupi le munthu.
Ajeremani atapita kumeneko ng’anga Basikolo Wadi Macheso sadalole kuwathandiza.
Powakanira chomwecho sindiye Ajeremani kwiyani.
Sindiye yamben kuiombera ng’anga.
Adaziona ana azungu kumeneko sindiye akuti zozwetetsa muntu paling arane zumana wa mrungu kui apo ndi ‘euphulites mfuti, ngfanga yachikudayo Iumangoseke.
Mifuti yalira koyamba ng’angayo yasanduka buluzi.
Khama la mzungu sinaiye amvekere ndiombera buluziyo, akatero angoona buluzi wasanduka njoka, kuombera loka angoona yasanduka khoswe, khoswe wasanduka ‘Rianhe, neemba yasanduka taache, taache lasanduke ‘munthu.
Uyo munthu ali apoyo, akungomwetulira.
Kumuombera munthu sadzagwa pansi.
Kenaka munthu wosafa nai kuomberedwayu adangoima njoo-Aksngoteokomola mkamwa mwake kutuluka njuchi, ndiyetu njuchi lumani Ajeremani, nkhope zawo tupani Aneto ndiye pomwe azungu adadziwa kuti munthu.

Zonsezitu nzomangoti akuti zidatere... akuti zidatere.
Akuluakulu clongosola nichanizi ena akuti adachita ‘kudzionera okhha, koma ambiri ndi onena kuti adauzidwa ndi makolo.
Chosangalatsa nchakuti ngakhale omwe ‘adachita kumva kuchokera kwa makolo, polongosola nkhanizi sikutsimikiza kwake.
Usati uwatsutse pena ake, achita kufuna kukumenya.
Iwo polongosola nkhanizi m'maso muli mbee ngati kuti adawaonadi Ajeremani akumuombera Chipolopolo.

Anasumbulera adakhala pansi ndipo a Kwapsa
adapitiriza kulankhula, “Abiti Joni omwe akhala
kkutsogolowo, amake a Zione, chiphadzuwa mukukwatitsa
Jerochi, timakhala nawo kunsi kwa mulatho mpaka lero
lino. Koma pali chinthu chimodzi chomvetsa chisoni.
Ndicho chakuti tate wake wa Zione ife sitimudziwa. Abiti
Joni adapezeka wodwala, koma adakana kutiuza mvini
pakatipo.”

Nthawi yomweyo Abiti Joni adanyamuka pampando
pomwe adakhalapo ndi kufwula, “Tate wa mwanayu
‘mumudziwa lero. Ndili ndi chithunzi chake, Ndachitenga
‘kuti ndimpatse Zione monga mphatso ya pa ukwati wake.

“Musadandaule abale anga, tate wa Zione mumuons
pachithunzi. Ndidakumana naye mwamunayu kamodzi.
Adandipatsa pakati ine osamudziwa, adandichita
chipongwe, Munthu wovutika ngati ine adangonditola
Panjira ndikuchokera kuganyu yosinja kumalaini,
nkundichita chipongwe, nkundithawa, Mwamwayi
wanga ndidamulanda jekete ndipo m'jeketemo
ndidapezamo chithunzi. Muchiona lero, Papita zaka
zambiri, taonani Zione lero walowa m’banja. Nyimbo
kumeneko abale anga a kunsi kwa mulatho.”
